Session Number: 70

Chapter: Chapter 5 : The Knight and the Dragon

Key Locations: the DMZ between Silverrige and Montimer

Media:

Glory Gains:

Players Attending:

- Jennifer Wolfe ([[siobhán_silverridge|Siobhán Silverridge]] / Amund Henge)
- Laura Bee ([[Lyla_Tarasovich-Talmert|Lyla_Tarasovich-Talmert]] /Soverighn Ides Lev Tarasovich)
- Damon Dewitt (Caden Mattix)
- Kenny Linden (Casimir Ramirez / [[Penelope-Durand|Penelope Durand]])
- Michael Kolb (Peter MacBravo)

---

# Synopsis

1. Almerin holds animosity towards Montimier, possibly due to a desire to harm them.
2. Peter MacBravo engages in friendly banter with an old woman named Nenetl and learns a Saltblood saying from her.
3. Peter's fiancée disagrees with his plan to involve Montimier in navigating to Bellkind.
4. She shares a vision suggesting that marrying Peter will cause significant changes in the Empire or Montimier.
5. Casimir and Lyla discuss potential dangers in Montimier and the need to be flexible in their plans.
6. The group is attacked by shadowy men resembling Clemente, but their motives remain unclear.
7. The attackers seem associated with the Camp Followers of Hussars.
8. The group discovers an ancient creature in an Esten temple, and Shiobhan has a cryptic conversation with it.
9. The creature indicates that using a specific tree symbol as a banner is crucial to avoiding betrayal.
10. Casimir removes a curse through communing with the Bellringer, resulting in the appearance of a dagger.
11. Lyla undergoes a transformation in the temple, becoming a full Esten.
12. Casimir talks with Pavel, who is fighting demons, and Siobhan learns that Hailey got close to a cure.
13. Peter finds out that Endy's right-hand man knows his identity, but his father didn't.
14. In Garzonet, Lyla discovers that the tree spirit is a "Grandmother" and meets Daniel and Irma Eisenberg.
15. The group requests an audience with the Eisenbergs to discuss Montimier and faces questions about alliances.
16. The next game will involve a discussion with Maisy.
